#################################### Minerals ########################################
defined_text = {
    name = cheatinterface_2_minerals_title
    text = {
        trigger = {
            NOT = {
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t1_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t2_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t3_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t4_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t5_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t6_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t7_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t8_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t9_modifier
                has_country_flag = cheatinterface_has_resource_minerals_t10_modifier

            }
        }
        localization_key = cheatinterface_2_minerals
    }
    text = {
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t1
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t2
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t3
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t4
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t5
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t6
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t7
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t8
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t9
                has_modifier = cheatinterface_resource_minerals_t10
            }
        }
        localization_key = cheatinterface_2_minerals_b
    }
}
